569→    results: list[StepResult],\n   570→    remediate_metadata: dict | None = None,\n   571→    certify_metadata: dict | None = None,\n   572→) -> None:\n   573→    \"\"\"Write .roadmap-state.json Check if the output indicates degraded mode\n   644→        if result.step and result.step.output_file.exists():\n   645→            content = result.step.output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   646→            if \"validation_complete: false\" in content:\n   647→                return \"degraded\"\n   648→        return \"pass\"\n   649→    if result.status == StepStatus.SKIPPED:\n   650→        return \"skipped\"\n   651→    if result.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT):\n   652→        return \"fail\"\n   653→    return \"skipped\"\n   654→\n   655→\n   656→def generate_degraded_report(\n   657→    output_file: Path,\n   658→    failed_agent: str,\n   659→    failure_reason: str,\n   660→) -> None:\n   661→    \"\"\"Generate a degraded fidelity report when the agent fails.\n   662→\n   663→    Produces a report with validation_complete=false and\n   664→    fidelity_check_attempted=true so the SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE\n   665→    can distinguish degraded from clean passes (NFR-007).\n   666→\n   667→    The degraded report names the failed agent and reason in the body.\n   668→    \"\"\"\n   669→    report = (\n   670→        \"---\\n\"\n   671→        \"high_severity_count: 0\\n\"\n   672→        \"medium_severity_count: 0\\n\"\n   673→        \"low_severity_count: 0\\n\"\n   674→        \"total_deviations: 0\\n\"\n   675→        \"validation_complete: false\\n\"\n   676→        \"fidelity_check_attempted: true\\n\"\n   677→        \"tasklist_ready: false\\n\"\n   678→        \"---\\n\"\n   679→        \"\\n\"\n   680→        \"## Degraded Fidelity Report\\n\"\n   681→        \"\\n\"\n   682→        \"Spec-fidelity validation could not be completed.\\n\"\n   683→        \"\\n\"\n   684→        f\"**Failed Agent**: {failed_agent}\\n\"\n   685→        f\"**Failure Reason**: {failure_reason}\\n\"\n   686→        \"\\n\"\n   687→        \"This is a degraded report produced after agent failure and retry \"\n   688→        \"exhaustion. derive_pipeline_status(state: dict) -> str:\n   754→    \"\"\"Derive the overall pipeline status from state transitions.\n   755→\n   756→    State transitions at each boundary:\n   757→    - post-validate: validated | validated-with-issues\n   758→    - post-remediate: remediated\n   759→    - post-certify: certified | certified-with-caveats\n   760→\n   761→    Returns one of: 'pending', 804→        return None\n   805→\n   806→\n   807→def apply_decomposition_pass(deliverables: list[Deliverable]) -> list[Deliverable]:\n   808→    \"\"\"Post-generation decomposition pass for the 822→def execute_roadmap(config: RoadmapConfig, resume: bool = False, no_validate: bool = False) -> None:\n   823→    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n   824→\n   825→    Builds the step Returns False on mismatch\n    (fail closed).\n    \"\"\"\n    from .gates import _parse_frontmatter\n\n    content = tasklist_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    fm = _parse_frontmatter(content)\n    if fm is None:\n        return False\n\n    saved_hash = fm.get(\"source_report_hash\", \"\")\n    if not saved_hash:\n        return False\n\n    # Find the validation report (source_report field)\n    source_report = fm.get(\"source_report\", \"\")\n    if source_report:\n        report_path = Path(source_report)\n        if not report_path.is_absolute():\n            report_path = output_dir / report_path\n    else:\n        # Default to reflect-merged.md or merged-validation-report.md\n        report_path = output_dir / \"reflect-merged.md\"\n        if not report_path.exists():\n            report_path = output_dir / \"merged-validation-report.md\"\n\n    if not report_path.exists():\n        return False\n\n    current_hash = hashlib.sha256(report_path.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n    return saved_hash == current_hash\n\n\ndef _apply_resume(\n    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    gate_fn: Callable,\n) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n    \"\"\"Apply --resume logic: skip steps whose outputs already pass gates.\n\n    Also checks for stale spec detection.\n    \"\"\"\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n    force_extract = False\n    if state is not None:\n        saved_hash = state.get(\"spec_hash\", \"\")\n        current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n        if saved_hash and saved_hash != current_hash:\n            print(\n                f\"WARNING: spec-file has changed since last run.\\n\"\n                f\"  Last hash: {saved_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n                f\"  Current:   {current_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n                f\"Forcing re-run of extract step.\",\n                file=sys.stderr,\n                flush=True,\n            )\n            force_extract = True\n\n    skipped = 0\n    result: list[Step | list[Step]] = []\n    found_failure = False\n\n    for entry in steps:\n        if found_failure:\n            # After first failing step, include all remaining steps\n            result.append(entry)\n            continue\n\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            # Parallel group: check all steps\n            all_pass = True\n            for s in entry:\n                if s.gate:\n                    passed, _reason = gate_fn(s.output_file, s.gate)\n                    if not passed:\n                        all_pass = False\n                        break\n                else:\n                    all_pass = False\n                    break\n            if all_pass:\n                skipped += len(entry)\n                print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {', '.join(s.id for s in entry)} (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n            else:\n                found_failure = True\n                result.append(entry)\n        else:\n            # \"\"\"Extract lines around a range with context window.\"\"\"\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    # Convert to 0-indexed\n    actual_start = max(0, start - 1 - context)\n    actual_end = \"\"\"Edge cases: SIGINT recovery, out-of-allowlist, zero-findings, fallback parser.\"\"\"\n\n    # --- Edge Case 1: SIGINT leaves .pre-remediate files ---\n\n    def test_sigint_leaves_snapshots_for_recovery(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"SIGINT during remediation: .pre-remediate files remain for manual recovery.\"\"\"\n        target = tmp_path / \"roadmap.md\"\n        target.write_text(\"# Original content\\n\")\n\n        # Create snapshots\n        snapshot_paths = create_snapshots([str(target)])\n        assert len(snapshot_paths) == 1\n\n        snapshot = Path(snapshot_paths[0])\n        assert snapshot.exists()\n        assert snapshot.read_text() == \"# Original content\\n\"\n\n        # Simulate: file modified during remediation\n        target.write_text(\"# Modified by agent\\n\")\n\n        # Simulate SIGINT: don't call cleanup_snapshots\n        # Verify snapshot still exists for manual recovery\n        assert snapshot.exists()\n        assert snapshot.read_text() == \"# Original content\\n\"\n\n        # Manual recovery possible via restore\n        restore_from_snapshots([str(target)])\n        assert target.read_text() == \"# Original content\\n\"\n\n    def test_snapshot_restore_atomicity(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Restore uses os.replace() for atomicity.\"\"\"\n        target = tmp_path / \"roadmap.md\"\n        target.write_text(\"# Original\\n\")\n        create_snapshots([str(target)])\n\n        target.write_text(\"# Modified\\n\")\n        restore_from_snapshots([str(target)])\n\n        assert target.read_text() == \"# Original\\n\"\n        # Snapshot consumed by restore\n        assert not
